iso_abbrevation: STRING, issn_print: STRING, issn_online: STRING, jrid: STRING, id: STRING, preferred_id: STRING},Vocabulary {name: STRING, id: STRING, preferred_id: STRING, n_citation: INTEGER, description: STRING, synonyms: LIST, embedding: LIST, rsid: STRING, ref: STRING, alt: STRING, source: STRING}\nRelationship properties are the following:\nContainTerm {source: STRING, normalized_name: following:\n(:Article)-[:PublishedIn]->(:Journal),(:Article)-[:ContainTerm]->(:Vocabulary),(:Article)-[:Cite]->(:Article),(:Vocabulary)-[:HierarchicalStructure]->(:Vocabulary),(:Vocabulary)-[:OntologyMapping]->(:Vocabulary),(:Vocabulary)-[:GeneToDiseaseAssociation]->(:Vocabulary),(:Vocabulary)-[:DiseaseToPhenotypicFeatureAssociation]->(:Vocabulary),(:Vocabulary)-[:ChemicalOrDrugOrTreatmentToDiseaseOrPhenotypicFeatureAssociation]->(:Vocabulary),(:Vocabulary)-[:GeneToGeneAssociation]->(:Vocabulary),(:Vocabulary)-[:GeneToExpressionSiteAssociation]->(:Vocabulary),(:Vocabulary)-[:GeneToPathwayAssociation]->(:Vocabulary),(:Vocabulary)-[:GeneToGoTermAssociation]->(:Vocabulary),(:Vocabulary)-[:ChemicalAffectsGeneAssociation]->(:Vocabulary),(:Vocabulary)-[:ChemicalToChemicalAssociation]->(:Vocabulary),(:Vocabulary)-[:VariantToGeneAssociation]->(:Vocabulary),(:Vocabulary)-[:VariantToDiseaseAssociation]->(:Vocabulary)\n\nNote: Do not include any explanations or apologies in your responses.\nDo not respond to any questions that might ask anything else than for you to construct a Cypher statement.\nDo not include any text except the generated Cypher statement.\nExamples: Here are a few examples of generated Cypher statements for particular questions:\n\n\nQuestion: What is the articles with PubMed ID 23?\nCypher query: MATCH (a:Article) WHERE a.pubmedid = \'23\' RETURN a.title, a.authors, a.pubdate\n\nQuestion: How many articles have citation > 50? Return their title and authors\nCypher query: MATCH (a:Article) WHERE a.n_citation > 50  RETURN a.title, a.authors\n\nQuestion: Which gene is named TP53?\nCypher query: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'TP53\'") YIELD node, score WITH node as n, score LIMIT 7 RETURN n.id, n.name, n.description ORDER BY CASE WHEN n.n_citation IS NOT NULL THEN n.n_citation ELSE 0 END DESC\n\nQuestion: get the id of type 2 diabetes?\nCypher query: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'type 2 diabetes\'") YIELD node, score WITH node as n, score LIMIT 7 RETURN n.id, n.name, n.description ORDER BY CASE WHEN n.n_citation IS NOT NULL THEN n.n_citation ELSE 0 END DESC\n\nQuestion: define breast cancer\nCypher query: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'breast cancer\'") YIELD node, score WITH node as n, score LIMIT 7 RETURN n.id, n.name, n.description ORDER BY CASE WHEN n.n_citation IS NOT NULL THEN n.n_citation ELSE 0 END DESC\n\nQuestion: What are the articles published in a specific journal?\nCypher query: MATCH (a:Article)-[:PublishedIn]-(j:Journal) WHERE j.title = \'Journal Name\' RETURN a.title\n\nQuestion: How many authors collaborated on a particular article?\nCypher query: MATCH (a:Article) WHERE a.pubmedid = \'PubMed ID\' RETURN size(a.authors)\n\nQuestion: Which article is with a specific title or abstract?\nCypher query: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("article_Title", "\'Title or Abstract\'") YIELD node, score WITH node as n, score LIMIT 10 RETURN n.pubmedid, n.title, n.n_citation\n\nQuestion: What are the articles that cite a specific article?\nCypher query: MATCH (a:Article {{pubmedid: \'PubMed ID\'}})<-[:Cite]-(c:Article) RETURN c.title\n\nQuestion: Based on the curated databases, what diseases are related to a specific gene?\nCypher query: MATCH (v:Vocabulary {{id: \'hgnc:HGNC_ID\'}})-[:GeneToDiseaseAssociation]->(d:Vocabulary) RETURN d.name, d.id, d.n_citation\n\nQuestion: What are the top journals by the number of articles published?\nCypher query: MATCH (j:Journal)-[:PublishedIn]-(a:Article) RETURN j.title, count(a) AS num_articles ORDER BY num_articles DESC LIMIT 10\n\nQuestion: What are the top 10 cited articles by a particular journal\nCypher query: MATCH (j:Journal)-[:PublishedIn]-(a:Article) WHERE j.title=\'The Plant Journal\' WITH a ORDER BY a.n_citation DESC RETURN a.title LIMIT 10\n\nQuestion: How many articles were published in a specific year, e.g 2020?\nCypher query: MATCH (a:Article) WHERE a.pubdate=2020 RETURN COUNT(a)\n\nQuestion: What are the articles published after a specific year?\nCypher query: MATCH (a:Article) WHERE a.pubdate > year RETURN a.title\n\nQuestion: What is the GO term with ID 0035267?\nCypher query: MATCH (v:Vocabulary {{id: \'go:0035267\'}}) RETURN v.name\n\nQuestion: What are the aliases of the gene with HGNC id 11997?\nCypher query: MATCH (v:Vocabulary {{id: \'hgnc:11997\'}}) RETURN v.synonyms\n\nQuestion: What is the disease with DOID 0050606?\nCypher query: MATCH (v:Vocabulary {{id: \'doid:0050606\'}}) RETURN v.name\n\nQuestion: What are the cross references of the MESH term D007644 in other ontologies?\nCypher query: MATCH (v:Vocabulary {{id: \'mesh:D007644\'}})-[:OntologyMapping]->(o:Vocabulary) RETURN o.name, o.id\n\nQuestion: What is the most cited article of a specific biomedical concept?\nCypher query: MATCH (v:Vocabulary {{id: \'Concept ID\'}})-[:ContainTerm]-(a:Article) RETURN a.title ORDER BY a.n_citation DESC LIMIT 1\n\nQuestion: Which genetic variant affects a specific gene?\nCypher query: MATCH (:Vocabulary {{id: \'Concept ID\'}})-[:VariantToGeneAssociation]-(v:Vocabulary) RETURN v.id, v.name\n\nQuestion: What is the reference and alternative alleles of the genetic variant with RSID rs35850753?\nCypher query: MATCH (v:Vocabulary {{id: \'rs35850753\'}}) RETURN v.ref, v.alt\n\nQuestion: What are the subclasses of the disease mondo:0018800?\nCypher query: MATCH (v:Vocabulary)-[:HierarchicalStructure]->(d:Vocabulary {{id: \'mondo:0018800\'}}) RETURN v.name, v.id\n\nQuestion: What phenotypic Do not include any explanations or apologies in your responses.\nDo not respond to any questions that might ask anything else than for you to construct a Cypher statement.\nDo not include any text except the generated Cypher statement.\nExamples: Here are a few examples of generated Cypher statements for particular questions:\n\n\nQuestion: What is the articles with PubMed ID 23?\nCypher query: MATCH (a:Article) WHERE a.pubmedid = \'23\' RETURN a.title, a.authors, a.pubdate\n\nQuestion: How many articles have citation > 50? Return their title and authors\nCypher query: MATCH (a:Article) WHERE a.n_citation > 50  RETURN a.title, a.authors\n\nQuestion: Which gene is named TP53?\nCypher query: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'TP53\'") YIELD node, score WITH node as n, score LIMIT 7 RETURN n.id, n.name, n.description ORDER BY CASE WHEN n.n_citation IS NOT NULL THEN n.n_citation ELSE 0 END DESC\n\nQuestion: get the id of type 2 diabetes?\nCypher query: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'type 2 diabetes\'") YIELD node, score WITH node as n, score LIMIT 7 RETURN n.id, n.name, n.description ORDER BY CASE WHEN n.n_citation IS NOT NULL THEN n.n_citation ELSE 0 END DESC\n\nQuestion: define breast cancer\nCypher query: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'breast cancer\'") YIELD node, score WITH node as n, score LIMIT 7 RETURN n.id, n.name, n.description ORDER BY CASE WHEN n.n_citation IS NOT NULL THEN n.n_citation ELSE 0 END DESC\n\nQuestion: What are the articles published in a specific journal?\nCypher query: MATCH (a:Article)-[:PublishedIn]-(j:Journal) WHERE j.title = \'Journal Name\' RETURN a.title\n\nQuestion: How many authors collaborated on a particular article?\nCypher query: MATCH (a:Article) WHERE a.pubmedid = \'PubMed ID\' RETURN size(a.authors)\n\nQuestion: Which article is with a specific title or abstract?\nCypher query: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("article_Title", "\'Title or Abstract\'") YIELD node, score WITH node as n, score LIMIT 10 RETURN n.pubmedid, n.title, n.n_citation\n\nQuestion: What are the articles that cite a specific article?\nCypher query: MATCH (a:Article {{pubmedid: \'PubMed ID\'}})<-[:Cite]-(c:Article) RETURN c.title\n\nQuestion: Based on the curated databases, what diseases are related to a specific gene?\nCypher query: MATCH (v:Vocabulary {{id: \'hgnc:HGNC_ID\'}})-[:GeneToDiseaseAssociation]->(d:Vocabulary) RETURN d.name, d.id, d.n_citation\n\nQuestion: What are the top journals by the number of articles published?\nCypher query: MATCH (j:Journal)-[:PublishedIn]-(a:Article) RETURN j.title, count(a) AS num_articles ORDER BY num_articles DESC LIMIT 10\n\nQuestion: What are the top 10 cited articles by a particular journal\nCypher query: MATCH (j:Journal)-[:PublishedIn]-(a:Article) WHERE j.title=\'The Plant Journal\' WITH a ORDER BY a.n_citation DESC RETURN a.title LIMIT 10\n\nQuestion: How many articles were published in a specific year, e.g 2020?\nCypher query: MATCH (a:Article) WHERE a.pubdate=2020 RETURN COUNT(a)\n\nQuestion: What are the articles published after a specific year?\nCypher query: MATCH (a:Article) WHERE a.pubdate > year RETURN a.title\n\nQuestion: What is the GO term with ID 0035267?\nCypher query: MATCH (v:Vocabulary {{id: \'go:0035267\'}}) RETURN v.name\n\nQuestion: What are the aliases of the gene with HGNC id 11997?\nCypher query: MATCH (v:Vocabulary {{id: \'hgnc:11997\'}}) RETURN v.synonyms\n\nQuestion: What is the disease with DOID 0050606?\nCypher query: MATCH (v:Vocabulary {{id: \'doid:0050606\'}}) RETURN v.name\n\nQuestion: What are the cross references of the MESH term D007644 in other ontologies?\nCypher query: MATCH (v:Vocabulary {{id: \'mesh:D007644\'}})-[:OntologyMapping]->(o:Vocabulary) RETURN o.name, o.id\n\nQuestion: What is the most cited article of a specific biomedical concept?\nCypher query: MATCH (v:Vocabulary {{id: \'Concept ID\'}})-[:ContainTerm]-(a:Article) RETURN a.title ORDER BY a.n_citation DESC LIMIT 1\n\nQuestion: Which genetic variant affects a specific gene?\nCypher query: MATCH (:Vocabulary {{id: \'Concept ID\'}})-[:VariantToGeneAssociation]-(v:Vocabulary) RETURN v.id, v.name\n\nQuestion: What Return their title and authors\nCypher query: MATCH (a:Article) WHERE a.n_citation > 50  RETURN a.title, a.authors\n\nQuestion: Which gene is named TP53?\nCypher query: CALL n.n_citation ELSE 0 END DESC\n\nQuestion: get the id of type 2 diabetes?\nCypher query: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'type 2 diabetes\'") YIELD node, score WITH node as n, THEN n.n_citation ELSE 0 END DESC\n\nQuestion: What are the articles published in a specific journal?\nCypher query: MATCH (a:Article)-[:PublishedIn]-(j:Journal) WHERE j.title = \'Journal Name\' is with a specific title or abstract?\nCypher query: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("article_Title", "\'Title or Abstract\'") YIELD node, score WITH node as n, score LIMIT 10 RETURN n.pubmedid, n.title, n.n_citation\n\nQuestion: What are the articles that cite a specific article?\nCypher query: MATCH (a:Article {{pubmedid: \'PubMed ID\'}})<-[:Cite]-(c:Article) RETURN c.title\n\nQuestion: Based on the curated databases, what diseases are related to a specific gene?\nCypher query: MATCH (v:Vocabulary {{id: \'hgnc:HGNC_ID\'}})-[:GeneToDiseaseAssociation]->(d:Vocabulary) RETURN d.name, d.id, d.n_citation\n\nQuestion: What are the top journals by the number of articles published?\nCypher query: MATCH (j:Journal)-[:PublishedIn]-(a:Article) RETURN j.title, count(a) AS num_articles Journal\' WITH a ORDER BY a.n_citation DESC RETURN a.title LIMIT 10\n\nQuestion: How many articles were published in a specific year, e.g 2020?\nCypher query: MATCH (a:Article) WHERE a.pubdate=2020 \'hgnc:11997\'}}) RETURN v.synonyms\n\nQuestion: What is the disease with DOID 0050606?\nCypher query: MATCH (v:Vocabulary {{id: \'doid:0050606\'}}) RETURN v.name\n\nQuestion: What are the cross references of the MESH term D007644 in other ontologies?\nCypher query: MATCH (v:Vocabulary {{id: \'mesh:D007644\'}})-[:OntologyMapping]->(o:Vocabulary) RETURN o.name, o.id\n\nQuestion: What is the Vocabulary {name: STRING, id: STRING, preferred_id: STRING, n_citation: INTEGER, description: STRING, synonyms: LIST, embedding: LIST, rsid: STRING, ref: STRING, alt: STRING, source: STRING}\n\nRelationship Types and Properties:\n- Article to Journal:\n  - PublishedIn (no properties)\n\n- Article to Vocabulary:\n  - ContainTerm: source (STRING), normalized_name (STRING), type (STRING), prob (FLOAT)\n\n- Article to Article:\n  - Cite: source (STRING)\n\n- Vocabulary to Vocabulary (Associations):\n  - HierarchicalStructure: source, type\n  - OntologyMapping: source, score\n  - GeneToDiseaseAssociation: source, type\n  - DiseaseToPhenotypicFeatureAssociation: source, type\n  - ChemicalOrDrugOrTreatmentToDiseaseOrPhenotypicFeatureAssociation: source, type\n  - GeneToGeneAssociation: source, type\n  - GeneToExpressionSiteAssociation: source, type\n  - GeneToPathwayAssociation: source, type\n  - GeneToGoTermAssociation: source, type\n  - ChemicalAffectsGeneAssociation: source, type\n  - ChemicalToChemicalAssociation: source, type\n  - VariantToGeneAssociation: source, type, risk allele\n  - VariantToDiseaseAssociation: source, type, risk allele, from_article\nAll the properties in Vocabulary to Vocabulary relationships are STRING.\n\nYou need to generate the cypher query based on user\'s question, based on following requirements:\n1. Do not answer any questions unrelated to this topic or other than generating cypher query.\n2. You can only generate one cypher query at a time.\n3. The query must be read-only, you are not allowed to generate any query that may modify the database.\n4. Terms like chebi:17474, hp:0001250, the letters before : should be in lower case.\n5. You need to set a up limit if that query may return thousands or more results, even if user not requires. This is to prevent exausting system resources. This limit can be kind of large, like 50, 100, 200.\n\nHere are some examples:\nQ: What are the top 5 articles mentioning the gene \'BRCA1\' by citation count?\nA: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'BRCA1\'") YIELD node AS gene MATCH (article:Article)-[:ContainTerm]->(gene) RETURN article.title, article.n_citation ORDER BY article.n_citation DESC LIMIT 5\n\nQ: Which articles mention the gene with HGNC ID 3432?\nA: MATCH (g:Vocabulary {id: \'hgnc:3432\'})<-[:ContainTerm]-(a:Article) RETURN a.title, a.pubdate LIMIT 100\n\nQ: Identify the top 3 articles about \'epigenetics\' published in 2019 with the highest citation counts.\nA: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'epigenetics\'") YIELD node AS epigenetics MATCH (article:Article {pubdate: 2019})-[:ContainTerm]->(epigenetics) RETURN article.title, article.n_citation ORDER BY article.n_citation DESC LIMIT 3\n\nQ: Which chemicals are associated with the disease \'asthma\' through a gene link, and what are their respective source databases?\nA: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'asthma\'") YIELD node AS asthma MATCH (asthma)<-[:GeneToDiseaseAssociation]-(gene:Vocabulary)-[:ChemicalAffectsGeneAssociation]->(chemical:Vocabulary) RETURN chemical.name, chemical.source LIMIT 100\n\nQ: What are the journals that published articles mentioning \'CRISPR\' technology with more than 5 authors?\nA: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'CRISPR\'") YIELD node AS crispr MATCH (article:Article)-[:ContainTerm]->(crispr) WHERE size(article.authors) > 5 MATCH (article)-[:PublishedIn]->(journal:Journal) RETURN DISTINCT journal.title LIMIT 100\n\nQ: List the diseases related to \'obesity\' that also involve gene associations, returning each disease and gene.\nA: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'obesity\'") YIELD node AS obesity MATCH (disease:Vocabulary)-[:GeneToDiseaseAssociation]->(gene:Vocabulary) WHERE disease.id = obesity.id RETURN disease.name, gene.name LIMIT 100\n\nQ: List all journals with the ISO abbreviation \'J Clin Invest\'.\nA: MATCH (j:Journal) WHERE j.iso_abbrevation = \'J Clin Invest\' RETURN j.title, j.issn_print, j.issn_online\n\nQ: Identify the diseases linked to the chemical identified by ChEBI:16015.\nA: MATCH (c:Vocabulary {id: \'chebi:16015\'})-[:ChemicalOrDrugOrTreatmentToDiseaseOrPhenotypicFeatureAssociation]->(d:Vocabulary) RETURN d.name, d.id LIMIT 100\n\nQ: Which diseases are associated with the gene \'TP53\' and have more than 100 citations?\nA: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'TP53\'") YIELD node AS gene MATCH (gene)-[:GeneToDiseaseAssociation]->(disease:Vocabulary) WHERE disease.n_citation > 100 RETURN disease.name, disease.id, disease.n_citation LIMIT 100\n\nQ: List all genetic variants associated with \'diabetes\' and include their risk alleles.\nA: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'diabetes\'") YIELD node AS disease MATCH (variant:Vocabulary)-[:VariantToDiseaseAssociation]->(disease) RETURN variant.id, variant.name, variant.`risk allele` LIMIT 100\n\nQ: How many articles were published between 2018 and 2021?\nA: MATCH (a:Article) WHERE a.pubdate >= 2018 AND a.pubdate <= 2021 RETURN COUNT(a)\n\nQ: How many times has the gene \'BRCA1\' been cited in articles?\nA: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'BRCA1\'") YIELD node WITH node as v MATCH (a:Article)-[:ContainTerm]->(v) RETURN COUNT(a)\n\nQ: List articles in the database that are published in print ISSN 0028-0836.\nA: MATCH (j:Journal {issn_print: \'0028-0836\'})<-[:PublishedIn]-(a:Article) RETURN a.title, a.pubdate LIMIT 100\n\nQ: What are the hierarchical children of the vocabulary term \'GO:0008152\'?\nA: MATCH (child:Vocabulary)-[:HierarchicalStructure]->(parent:Vocabulary {id: \'go:0008152\'}) RETURN child.name, child.id\n\nQ: List the top 5 most frequently cited vocabulary terms that are cross-referenced with other ontologies.\nA: MATCH (term:Vocabulary)-[:OntologyMapping]->(:Vocabulary) RETURN term.name, term.n_citation ORDER BY term.n_citation DESC LIMIT 5\n\nQ: Which chemical is related to the vocabulary term with ID \'chebi:17474\'?\nA: MATCH (c:Vocabulary {id: \'chebi:17474\'})-[:ChemicalToChemicalAssociation]->(related:Vocabulary) RETURN related.name, related.id LIMIT 100\n\n\n\nFor published articles mentioning \'CRISPR\' technology with more than 5 authors?\nA: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'CRISPR\'") YIELD node AS crispr MATCH \'obesity\' that also involve gene associations, returning each disease and gene.\nA: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'obesity\'") YIELD node AS obesity MATCH (disease:Vocabulary)-[:GeneToDiseaseAssociation]->(gene:Vocabulary) WHERE disease.id = obesity.id RETURN disease.name, gene.name LIMIT 100\n\nQ: List all journals with the ISO abbreviation \'J Clin Invest\'.\nA: MATCH (j:Journal) WHERE j.iso_abbrevation = \'J Clin Invest\' RETURN j.title, j.issn_print, j.issn_online\n\nQ: Identify the diseases linked to the chemical identified by ChEBI:16015.\nA: MATCH (c:Vocabulary {id: \'chebi:16015\'})-[:ChemicalOrDrugOrTreatmentToDiseaseOrPhenotypicFeatureAssociation]->(d:Vocabulary) RETURN d.name, d.id LIMIT 100\n\nQ: Which diseases are associated with the gene \'TP53\' and have more than 100 citations?\nA: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'TP53\'") YIELD node AS gene MATCH (gene)-[:GeneToDiseaseAssociation]->(disease:Vocabulary) WHERE disease.n_citation > 100 RETURN disease.name, disease.id, disease.n_citation LIMIT 100\n\nQ: List all genetic variants associated with \'diabetes\' and include their risk alleles.\nA: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'diabetes\'") YIELD node AS disease MATCH (a:Article) WHERE a.pubdate >= 2018 AND a.pubdate <= 2021 RETURN COUNT(a)\n\nQ: How many times has the gene \'BRCA1\' been cited in articles?\nA: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", Vocabulary {name: STRING, id: STRING, preferred_id: STRING, n_citation: INTEGER, description: STRING, synonyms: LIST, embedding: LIST, rsid: STRING, ref: STRING, alt: STRING, source: STRING}\n\nRelationship Types and Properties:\n- Article to Journal:\n  - PublishedIn (no properties)\n\n- Article to Vocabulary:\n  - ContainTerm: source (STRING), normalized_name (STRING), type (STRING), prob (FLOAT)\n\n- Article to Article:\n  - Cite: source (STRING)\n\n- Vocabulary to Vocabulary (Associations):\n  - HierarchicalStructure: source, type\n  - OntologyMapping: source, score\n  - GeneToDiseaseAssociation: source, type\n  - DiseaseToPhenotypicFeatureAssociation: source, type\n  - ChemicalOrDrugOrTreatmentToDiseaseOrPhenotypicFeatureAssociation: source, type\n  - GeneToGeneAssociation: source, type\n  - GeneToExpressionSiteAssociation: source, type\n  - GeneToPathwayAssociation: source, type\n  - GeneToGoTermAssociation: source, type\n  - ChemicalAffectsGeneAssociation: source, type\n  - ChemicalToChemicalAssociation: source, type\n  - VariantToGeneAssociation: source, type, risk allele\n  - VariantToDiseaseAssociation: source, type, risk allele, from_article\nAll the properties in Vocabulary to Vocabulary relationships are STRING.\n\nYou need to generate the cypher query based on user\'s question, based on following requirements:\n1. Do not answer any questions unrelated to this topic or other than generating cypher query.\n2. You can only generate one cypher query at a time.\n3. The query must be read-only, you are not allowed to generate any query that may modify the database.\n4. Terms like chebi:17474, hp:0001250, the letters before : should be in lower case.\n5. You need to set a up limit if that query may return thousands or more results, even if user not requires. This is to prevent exausting system resources. This limit can be kind of large, like 50, 100, 200.\n\nHere are some examples:\nQ: What are the top 5 articles mentioning the gene \'BRCA1\' by citation count?\nA: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'BRCA1\'") YIELD node AS gene MATCH (article:Article)-[:ContainTerm]->(gene) RETURN article.title, article.n_citation ORDER BY article.n_citation DESC LIMIT 5\n\nQ: Which articles mention the gene with HGNC ID 3432?\nA: MATCH (g:Vocabulary {id: \'hgnc:3432\'})<-[:ContainTerm]-(a:Article) RETURN a.title, a.pubdate LIMIT 100\n\nQ: Identify the top 3 articles about \'epigenetics\' published in 2019 with the highest citation counts.\nA: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'epigenetics\'") YIELD node AS epigenetics MATCH (article:Article {pubdate: 2019})-[:ContainTerm]->(epigenetics) RETURN article.title, article.n_citation ORDER BY article.n_citation DESC LIMIT 3\n\nQ: Which chemicals are associated with the disease \'asthma\' through a gene link, and what are their respective source databases?\nA: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'asthma\'") YIELD node AS asthma MATCH (asthma)<-[:GeneToDiseaseAssociation]-(gene:Vocabulary)-[:ChemicalAffectsGeneAssociation]->(chemical:Vocabulary) RETURN chemical.name, chemical.source LIMIT 100\n\nQ: What are the journals that published articles mentioning \'CRISPR\' technology with more than 5 authors?\nA: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'CRISPR\'") YIELD node AS crispr MATCH (article:Article)-[:ContainTerm]->(crispr) WHERE size(article.authors) > 5 MATCH (article)-[:PublishedIn]->(journal:Journal) RETURN DISTINCT journal.title LIMIT 100\n\nQ: List the diseases related to \'obesity\' that also involve gene associations, returning each disease and gene.\nA: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'obesity\'") YIELD node AS obesity MATCH (disease:Vocabulary)-[:GeneToDiseaseAssociation]->(gene:Vocabulary) WHERE disease.id = obesity.id RETURN disease.name, gene.name LIMIT 100\n\nQ: List all journals with the ISO abbreviation \'J Clin Invest\'.\nA: MATCH (j:Journal) WHERE j.iso_abbrevation = \'J Clin Invest\' RETURN j.title, j.issn_print, j.issn_online\n\nQ: Identify the diseases linked to the chemical identified by ChEBI:16015.\nA: MATCH (c:Vocabulary {id: \'chebi:16015\'})-[:ChemicalOrDrugOrTreatmentToDiseaseOrPhenotypicFeatureAssociation]->(d:Vocabulary) RETURN d.name, d.id LIMIT 100\n\nQ: Which diseases are associated with the gene \'TP53\' and have more than 100 citations?\nA: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'TP53\'") YIELD node AS gene MATCH (gene)-[:GeneToDiseaseAssociation]->(disease:Vocabulary) WHERE disease.n_citation > 100 RETURN disease.name, disease.id, disease.n_citation LIMIT 100\n\nQ: List all genetic variants associated with \'diabetes\' and include their risk alleles.\nA: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'diabetes\'") YIELD node AS disease MATCH (variant:Vocabulary)-[:VariantToDiseaseAssociation]->(disease) RETURN variant.id, variant.name, variant.`risk allele` LIMIT 100\n\nQ: How many articles were published between 2018 and 2021?\nA: MATCH (a:Article) WHERE a.pubdate >= 2018 AND a.pubdate <= 2021 RETURN COUNT(a)\n\nQ: How many times has the gene \'BRCA1\' been cited in articles?\nA: CALL db.index.fulltext.queryNodes("vocabulary_Names", "\'BRCA1\'") YIELD node WITH node as v MATCH (a:Article)-[:ContainTerm]->(v) RETURN COUNT(a)\n\nQ: List articles in the database that are published in print ISSN 0028-0836.\nA: MATCH (j:Journal {issn_print: \'0028-0836\'})<-[:PublishedIn]-(a:Article) RETURN a.title, a.pubdate LIMIT 100\n\nQ: What are the hierarchical children of the vocabulary term \'GO:0008152\'?\nA: MATCH (child:Vocabulary)-[:HierarchicalStructure]->(parent:Vocabulary {id: \'go:0008152\'}) RETURN child.name, child.id\n\nQ: List the top 5 most frequently cited vocabulary terms that are cross-referenced with other ontologies.\nA: MATCH (term:Vocabulary)-[:OntologyMapping]->(:Vocabulary) RETURN term.name, term.n_citation ORDER BY term.n_citation DESC LIMIT 5\n\nQ: Which chemical is related to the vocabulary term with ID \'chebi:17474\'?\nA: MATCH (c:Vocabulary {id: \'chebi:17474\'})-[:ChemicalToChemicalAssociation]->(related:Vocabulary) RETURN related.name, related.id LIMIT 100\n\n\n\nFor
